17 package org.http4s.ember.core.h2
18 
19 import cats._
20 import cats.effect._
21 import cats.effect.syntax.all._
22 import cats.syntax.all._
23 import fs2._
24 import fs2.io.IOException
25 import fs2.io.net._
26 import org.http4s._
27 import org.typelevel.ci._
28 import org.typelevel.log4cats.Logger
29 import scodec.bits._
30 
31 import scala.concurrent.duration._
32 
33 import H2Frame.Settings.ConnectionSettings.{default => defaultSettings}
34 
35 private[ember] object H2Server {
36 
37   /*
38   3 Mechanism into H2
39 
40   TlsContext => Yes => ALPN =>  h2       => HTTP2
41                                 http/1.1 => HTTP1
42                                 Nothing  => Http1
43                 No  =>                      Http1
44 
45   This is the tricky one, must read the initial bytes
46   if they are the prelude then upgrade, but only on when
47   the connection is first established
48 
49   Client Prelude Bytes                   => Http2 // Http2-prior-kno
50   checkConnectionPreface
51   Note: implementations that support HTTP/2 over TLS MUST use protocol
52     negotiation in TLS.
53     So if TLS is used then this method is not allowed.
54 
55 
56   H2c
57             Request
58             Connection: Upgrade, HTTP2-Settings
59             Upgrade: h2c
60             HTTP2-Settings: <base64url encoding of HTTP/2 SETTINGS payload>
61               =>
62                 HTTP/1.1 101 Switching Protocols
63                 Connection: Upgrade
64                 Upgrade: h2c
65 
66                 Socket                    => Http2
67 
68             Normal                        => Resp
69 
70    */
71 
72   private val upgradeResponse: Response[fs2.Pure] = Response(
73     status = Status.SwitchingProtocols,
74     httpVersion = HttpVersion.`HTTP/1.1`,
75     headers = Headers(
76       "connection" -> "Upgrade",
77       "upgrade" -> "h2c",
78     ),
79   )
80   // Apply this, if it ever becomes Some, then rather than the next request, become an h2 connection
81   def h2cUpgradeHttpRoute[F[_]: Concurrent]: HttpRoutes[F] =
82     cats.data.Kleisli[({ type L[A] = cats.data.OptionT[F, A] })#L, Request[F], Response[F]] {
83       (req: Request[F]) =>
84         val connectionCheck = req.headers
85           .get[org.http4s.headers.Connection]
86           .exists(connection =>
87             connection.values.contains_(ci"upgrade") && connection.values
88               .contains_(ci"http2-settings")
89           )
90 
91         // checks are cascading so we execute the least amount of work
92         // if there is no upgrade, which is the likely case.
93         val upgradeCheck = connectionCheck && {
94           req.headers
95             .get(ci"upgrade")
96             .exists(upgrade => upgrade.map(r => r.value).exists(_ === "h2c"))
97         }
98 
99         val settings: Option[H2Frame.Settings.ConnectionSettings] = if (upgradeCheck) {
100           req.headers
101             .get(ci"http2-settings")
102             .collectFirstSome(settings =>
103               settings.map(_.value).collectFirstSome { value =>
104                 for {
105                   bv <- ByteVector.fromBase64(value, Bases.Alphabets.Base64Url) // Base64 Url
106                   settings <- H2Frame.Settings
107                     .fromPayload(bv, 0, false)
108                     .toOption // This isn't an entire frame
109                   // It is Just the Payload section of the frame
110                 } yield H2Frame.Settings
111                   .updateSettings(settings, H2Frame.Settings.ConnectionSettings.default)
112               }
113             )
114         } else None
115         val upgrade = connectionCheck && upgradeCheck
116         (settings, upgrade) match {
117           case (Some(settings), true) =>
118             cats.data.OptionT.liftF(req.body.compile.to(ByteVector): F[ByteVector]).flatMap { bv =>
119               val newReq: Request[fs2.Pure] = Request[fs2.Pure](
120                 req.method,
121                 req.uri,
122                 HttpVersion.`HTTP/2`,
123                 req.headers,
124                 Stream.chunk(Chunk.byteVector(bv)),
125                 req.attributes,
126               )
127               cats.data.OptionT.some(
128                 upgradeResponse.covary[F].withAttribute(H2Keys.H2cUpgrade, (settings, newReq))
129               )
130             }
131 
132           case (_, _) => cats.data.OptionT.none
133         }
134     }
135 
136   def h2cUpgradeMiddleware[F[_]: Concurrent](app: HttpApp[F]): HttpApp[F] =
137     cats.data.Kleisli { (req: Request[F]) =>
138       h2cUpgradeHttpRoute
139         .run(req)
140         .getOrElseF(app.run(req))
141     }
142 
143   // Call on a new connection for http2-prior-knowledge
144   // If left 1.1 if right 2
145   def checkConnectionPreface[F[_]: MonadThrow](socket: Socket[F]): F[Either[ByteVector, Unit]] =
146     socket.read(Preface.clientBV.size.toInt).flatMap {
147       case Some(s) =>
148         val received = s.toByteVector
149         if (received == Preface.clientBV) Applicative[F].pure(Either.unit)
150         else Applicative[F].pure(Either.left(received))
151       case None =>
152         new IOException("Input Closed Before Receiving Data").raiseError
153     }
154 
155   // For Anything that is guaranteed to only be h2 this method will fail
156   // unless the connection preface is there. For example after ALPN negotiation
157   // on an SSL connection.
158   def requireConnectionPreface[F[_]: MonadThrow](socket: Socket[F]): F[Unit] =
159     checkConnectionPreface(socket).flatMap {
160       case Left(_) => new IllegalArgumentException("Invalid Connection Preface").raiseError
161       case Right(unit) => unit.pure[F]
162     }
163 
164   // This is the full h2 management of a socket
165   // AFTER the connection preface.
166   // allowing delegation
167   def fromSocket[F[_]](
168       socket: Socket[F],
169       httpApp: HttpApp[F],
170       localSettings: H2Frame.Settings.ConnectionSettings,
171       logger: Logger[F],
172       // Only Used for http1 upgrade where remote settings are provided prior to escalation
173       initialRemoteSettings: H2Frame.Settings.ConnectionSettings = defaultSettings,
174       initialRequest: Option[Request[fs2.Pure]] = None,
175   )(implicit F: Async[F]): Resource[F, Unit] = {
176     import cats.effect.kernel.instances.spawn._
177 
178     // h2c Initial Request Communication on h2c Upgrade
179     def sendInitialRequest(h2: H2Connection[F])(req: Request[Pure]): F[Unit] =
180       for {
181         h2Stream <- h2.initiateRemoteStreamById(1)
182         s <- h2Stream.state.modify { s =>
183           val x = s.copy(state = H2Stream.StreamState.HalfClosedRemote)
184           (x, x)
185         }
186         _ <- s.request.complete(Either.right(req))
187         er = Either.right(req.body.compile.to(fs2.Collector.supportsByteVector(ByteVector)))
188         _ <- s.readBuffer.offer(er)
189         _ <- s.writeBlock.complete(Either.right(()))
190       } yield ()
191 
192     def holdWhileOpen(stateRef: Ref[F, H2Connection.State[F]]): F[Unit] =
193       F.sleep(1.seconds) >> stateRef.get.map(_.closed).ifM(F.unit, holdWhileOpen(stateRef))
194 
195     for {
196       address <- Resource.eval(socket.remoteAddress)
197       (remotehost, remoteport) = (address.host, address.port)
198       ref <- Resource.eval(Concurrent[F].ref(Map[Int, H2Stream[F]]()))
199       initialWriteBlock <- Resource.eval(Deferred[F, Either[Throwable, Unit]])
200       stateRef <- Resource.eval(
201         Concurrent[F].ref(
202           H2Connection.State(
203             initialRemoteSettings,
204             defaultSettings.initialWindowSize.windowSize,
205             initialWriteBlock,
206             localSettings.initialWindowSize.windowSize,
207             0,
208             0,
209             false,
210             None,
211             None,
212           )
213         )
214       )
215       queue <- Resource.eval(cats.effect.std.Queue.unbounded[F, Chunk[H2Frame]]) // TODO revisit
216       hpack <- Resource.eval(Hpack.create[F])
217       settingsAck <- Resource.eval(
218         Deferred[F, Either[Throwable, H2Frame.Settings.ConnectionSettings]]
219       )
220       streamCreationLock <- Resource.eval(cats.effect.std.Semaphore[F](1))
221       // data <- Resource.eval(cats.effect.std.Queue.unbounded[F, Frame.Data])
222       created <- Resource.eval(cats.effect.std.Queue.unbounded[F, Int])
223       closed <- Resource.eval(cats.effect.std.Queue.unbounded[F, Int])
224 
225       h2 = new H2Connection(
226         remotehost,
227         remoteport,
228         H2Connection.ConnectionType.Server,
229         localSettings,
230         ref,
231         stateRef,
232         queue,
233         created,
234         closed,
235         hpack,
236         streamCreationLock.permit,
237         settingsAck,
238         ByteVector.empty,
239         socket,
240         logger,
241       )
242       _ <- h2.writeLoop.compile.drain.background
243       _ <- Resource.eval(
244         queue.offer(Chunk.singleton(H2Frame.Settings.ConnectionSettings.toSettings(localSettings)))
245       )
246       _ <- h2.readLoop.background
247 
248       _ <- Resource.eval(h2.settingsAck.get.rethrow)
249       // h2c Initial Request Communication on h2c Upgrade
250       _ <- Resource.eval(
251         initialRequest.traverse_(req => sendInitialRequest(h2)(req) >> created.offer(1))
252       )
253       _ <-
254         Stream
255           .fromQueueUnterminated(closed)
256           .map(i =>
257             Stream.eval(
258               // Max Time After Close We Will Still Accept Messages
259               (Temporal[F].sleep(1.seconds) >>
260                 ref.update(m => m - i)).timeout(15.seconds).attempt.start
261             )
262           )
263           .parJoin(localSettings.maxConcurrentStreams.maxConcurrency)
264           .compile
265           .drain
266           .background
267 
268       _ <-
269         Stream
270           .fromQueueUnterminated(created)
271           .map { i =>
272             val x: F[Unit] = for {
273               stream <- ref.get.map(_.get(i)).map(_.get) // FOLD
274               req <- stream.getRequest.map(_.covary[F].withBodyStream(stream.readBody))
275               resp <- httpApp(req)
276               _ <- stream.sendHeaders(PseudoHeaders.responseToHeaders(resp), false)
277               // Push Promises
278               pp = resp.attributes.lookup(H2Keys.PushPromises)
279               pushEnabled <- stateRef.get.map(_.remoteSettings.enablePush.isEnabled)
280               streams <- (Alternative[Option].guard(pushEnabled) >> pp).fold(
281                 Applicative[F].pure(List.empty[(Request[fs2.Pure], H2Stream[F])])
282               ) { l =>
283                 l.traverse { req =>
284                   streamCreationLock.permit.use[(Request[Pure], H2Stream[F])](_ =>
285                     h2.initiateLocalStream.flatMap { stream =>
286                       stream
287                         .sendPushPromise(i, PseudoHeaders.requestToHeaders(req))
288                         .map(_ => (req, stream))
289                     }
290                   )
291                 }
292               }
293               // _ <- Console.make[F].println("Writing Streams Commpleted")
294               responses <- streams.parTraverse { case (req, stream) =>
295                 for {
296                   resp <- httpApp(req.covary[F])
297                   // _ <- Console.make[F].println("Push Promise Response Completed")
298                   _ <- stream.sendHeaders(
299                     PseudoHeaders.responseToHeaders(resp),
300                     false,
301                   ) // PP Response
302                 } yield (resp.body, stream)
303               }
304 
305               _ <- responses.parTraverse { case (_, stream) =>
306                 resp.body.chunks
307                   .evalMap(c => stream.sendData(c.toByteVector, false))
308                   .compile
309                   .drain >> // PP Resp Body
310                   stream.sendData(ByteVector.empty, true)
311               }
312               trailers = resp.attributes.lookup(Message.Keys.TrailerHeaders[F])
313               _ <- resp.body.chunks.noneTerminate.zipWithNext
314                 .evalMap {
315                   case (Some(c), Some(Some(_))) => stream.sendData(c.toByteVector, false)
316                   case (Some(c), Some(None) | None) =>
317                     if (trailers.isDefined) stream.sendData(c.toByteVector, false)
318                     else stream.sendData(c.toByteVector, true)
319                   case (None, _) =>
320                     if (trailers.isDefined) Applicative[F].unit
321                     else stream.sendData(ByteVector.empty, true)
322                 }
323                 .compile
324                 .drain // Initial Resp Body
325               optTrailers <- trailers.sequence
326               optNel = optTrailers.flatMap(h =>
327                 h.headers.map(a => (a.name.toString.toLowerCase(), a.value, false)).toNel
328               )
329               _ <- optNel.traverse(nel => stream.sendHeaders(nel, true))
330             } yield ()
331             Stream.eval(x.attempt)
332 
333           }
334           .parJoin(localSettings.maxConcurrentStreams.maxConcurrency)
335           .compile
336           .drain
337           .onError { case e => logger.error(e)(s"Server Connection Processing Halted") }
338           .background
339 
340       _ <- Resource.eval(
341         stateRef.update(s => s.copy(writeWindow = s.remoteSettings.initialWindowSize.windowSize))
342       )
343       _ <- Resource.eval(holdWhileOpen(stateRef))
344     } yield ()
345   }
346 }
